### Response: Question: A coder has 1000 followers on Twitter. He gains 100 followers every day. How many followers will he have in 5 days? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: A 20-year-old man is 66 inches tall.  His 10-year-old brother is 2/3 his height.  How tall is the 10-year-old in feet? Solution: def solution():

    return result

### Instruction:
Write one math word problem and Python code with a commented out step-by-step
### Response: Question: A baker is making a 3-layer cake. The first layer is 10 inches in diameter. The second layer is 8 inches in diameter. The third layer is 6 inches in diameter. What is the volume of the cake? Solution: def solution():
    #The first layer is 10 inches in diameter
    layer_1_diameter = 10
    #The second layer is 8 inches in diameter
    layer_2_diameter = 8
    #The third layer is 6 inches in diameter
    layer_3_diameter = 6
    #The height of each layer is 4 inches
    layer_height = 4
    #The volume of a cylinder is pi * radius^2 * height
    #The radius of the first layer is 10/2 = <<10/2=5>>5 inches
    layer_1_radius = 5
    layer_1_volume = 3.14 * (layer_1_radius ** 2) * layer_height
    #The radius of the second layer is 8/2 = <<8/2=4>>4 inches
    layer_2_radius = 4
    layer_2_volume = 3.14 * (layer_2_radius ** 2) * layer_height
    #The radius of the third layer is 6/2 = <<6/2=3>>3 inches
    layer_3_radius = 3
    layer_3_volume = 3.14 * (layer_3_radius ** 2) * layer_height
    #The total volume is
    result = layer_1_volume + layer_2_volume + layer_3_volume
    return result

### Response: Question: The soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards. 6 of the players are defenders. The rest of the players are goalies. How many goalies are there? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #6 are defenders
    players_defenders = 6
    #The rest are goalies
    players_goalies = players_total - players_forwards - players_defenders
    result = players_goalies
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-pound sack of apples costs $22. A 20-pound sack of apples costs $44. How much will 30 pounds of apples cost? Solution: def solution():
    #10 pounds of apples cost $22
    apples_10_pounds = 22
    #20 pounds of apples cost $44
    apples_20_pounds = 44
    #The answer is
    result = (apples_20_pounds - apples_10_pounds) / 10 + apples_10_pounds
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-pound bag of apples has 40 apples. How many 10-pound bags of apples does it take to have 120 apples? Solution: def solution():

    #120 apples / 40 apples per 10 pounds = <<120/40=3>>3 10-pound bags of apples

    return result

### Response: Question: The Beverly Hills Hotel has 240 rooms. 70% of the rooms are occupied. How many rooms are unoccupied? Solution: def solution():
    #The hotel has 240 rooms
    rooms = 240
    #70% of the rooms are occupied
    occupancy_percent = 70
    #The answer is
    result = rooms * (1 - occupancy_percent / 100)
    return result

### Response: Question: The gym has 100 towels. 20% of the towels are white. 50% of the towels are blue. The rest of the towels are green. How many towels are green? Solution: def solution():
    #20% of the towels are white
    white_towels = 0.2 * 100
    #50% of the towels are blue
    blue_towels = 0.5 * 100
    #The rest are green
    green_towels = 100 - white_towels - blue_towels
    return green_towels

### Response: Question: A 1
### Response: Question: A 20-pound box of oranges has 280 oranges. A 10-pound box of oranges has 140 oranges. How many oranges can you get for $10? Solution: def solution():
    #A 20-pound box of oranges has 280 oranges
    oranges_20_pounds = 280
    #A 10-pound box of oranges has 140 oranges
    oranges_10_pounds = 140
    #The 20-pound box costs $20
    cost_20_pounds = 20
    #The 10-pound box costs $10
    cost_10_pounds = 10
    #The 20-pound box has
    oranges_20_pounds_per_dollar = oranges_20_pounds / cost_20_pounds
    #oranges per dollar. The 10-pound box has
    oranges_10_pounds_per_dollar = oranges_10_pounds / cost_10_pounds
    #oranges per dollar. The average is
    oranges_per_dollar = (oranges_20_pounds_per_dollar + oranges_10_pounds_per_dollar) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = oranges_per_dollar * 10
    return result

### Response: Question: A cafeteria has 200 hamburgers. It sells 90 hamburgers at lunch and 120 hamburgers at dinner. How many hamburgers are left? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: A candy store sells 12 chocolate bars and 8 bags of gummy bears. Each chocolate bar costs $2.50 and each bag of gummy bears costs $3. The candy store then buys 3 bags of licorice and 4 bags of jelly beans. Each bag of licorice costs $2 and each bag of jelly beans costs $1.50. How much money did the candy store spend? Solution: def solution():
    #The candy store sold 12 chocolate bars
    chocolate_bars = 12
    #Each chocolate bar costs $2.50
    chocolate_bar_cost = 2.5
    #The candy store sold 8 bags of gummy bears
    gummy_bears = 8
    #Each bag of gummy bears costs $3
    gummy_bear_cost = 3
    #The candy store then bought 3 bags of licorice
    licorice = 3
    #Each bag of licorice costs $2
    licorice_cost = 2
    #The candy store bought 4 bags of jelly beans
    jelly_beans = 4
    #Each bag of jelly beans costs $1.50
    jelly_bean_cost = 1.5
    #The answer is
    result = (chocolate_bars * chocolate_bar_cost) + (gummy_bears * gummy_bear_cost) - (licorice * licorice_cost) - (jelly_beans * jelly_bean_cost)
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces. 20% of the weight is from the packaging. How much does the soap itself weigh? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_weight = 4
    #20% of the weight is from the packaging
    packaging_weight = soap_weight * 0.2
    #The answer is
    result = soap_weight - packaging_weight
    return result

### Response: Question: A theater has 200 seats. 40% of the seats are occupied by men and 10% by children. The rest are occupied by women. How many women are in the theater? Solution: def solution():
    #The total number of people in a theater is 200
    people_total = 200
    #40% of the people are men
    men_percent = 0.4
    #10% are children
    children_percent = 0.1
    #The rest are women
    women_percent = 1 - men_percent - children_percent
    #The number of women is
    women = people_total * women_percent
    return women

### Response: Question: The soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards, 6 are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many players are midfielders and defenders? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #6 are midfielders
    players_midfielders = 6
    #The rest are defenders
    players_defenders = players_total - players_forwards - players_midfielders
    #The answer is
    result = players_midfielders + players_defenders
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces.  A bottle of detergent weighs 10 ounces.  A bottle of bleach weighs 8 ounces.  How much do 10 cakes of soap, 5 boxes of soap powder, 3 bottles of detergent, and 2 bottles of bleach weigh? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces
    soap_powder_weight = 16
    #A bottle of detergent weighs 10 ounces
    detergent_weight = 10
    #A bottle of bleach weighs 8 ounces
    bleach_weight = 8
    #10 cakes of soap weigh
    soap_cake_total = soap_cake_weight * 10
    #5 boxes of soap powder weigh
    soap_powder_total = soap_powder_weight * 5
    #3 bottles of detergent weigh
    detergent_total = detergent_weight * 3
    #2 bottles of bleach weigh
    bleach_total = bleach_weight * 2
    #The answer is
    result = soap_cake_total + soap_powder_total + detergent_total + bleach_total
    return result

### Response: Question: A baker is making a cake. The cake's recipe calls for 4.5 cups of flour. The baker has 1.5 cups of white flour and 2.5 cups of whole wheat flour. How many more cups of flour does the baker need? Solution: def solution():
    #The cake calls for 4.5 cups of flour
    flour_needed = 4.5
    #The baker has 1.5 cups of white flour
    flour_white = 1.5
    #The baker has 2.5 cups of whole wheat flour
    flour_wheat = 2.5
    #The baker has a total of
    flour_total = flour_white + flour_wheat
    #The baker needs
    result = flour_needed - flour_total
    return result
Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropri
### Response: Question: A baker has 200 muffins. He sells 1/4 of the muffins in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining muffins in the afternoon. How many muffins does he have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker has 200 muffins
    muffins = 200
    #1/4 of the muffins were sold in the morning
    muffins_sold_morning = muffins / 4
    #1/2 of the remaining muffins were sold in the afternoon
    muffins_sold_afternoon = (muffins - muffins_sold_morning) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = muffins - muffins_sold_morning - muffins_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: 123456789 is a 9-digit number. If you add the 1st, 3rd, and 5th digits, you get 1 + 3 + 5 = <<1+3+5=9>>9. If you add the 2nd, 4th, 6th, and 7th digits, you get 2 + 4 + 6 + 7 = <<2+4+6+7=19>>19. If you add the 8th and 9th digits, you get 8 + 9 = <<8+9=17>>17. The sum of all the digits is 9 + 19 + 17 = <<9+19+17=45>>45. What is the 8th digit of 123456789? Solution: def solution():
    #The 8th and 9th digits sum to 17
    digit_8_9 = 17
    #The 2nd, 4th, 6th, and 7th digits sum to 19
    digit_2_4_6_7 = 19
    #The 1st, 3rd, and 5th digits sum to 9
    digit_1_3_5 = 9
    #The sum of all the digits is 45
    digit_sum = 45
    #The 8th digit is
    result = digit_8_9 - 9
    return result

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards, 8 are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many players are defenders? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players = 24
    #12 are forwards
    forwards = 12
    #8 are midfielders
    midfielders = 8
    #The rest are defenders
    defenders = players - forwards - midfielders
    return defenders

### Response: Question: A baker has 240 muffins. She sells 1/3 of the muffins in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining muffins in the afternoon. How many muffins does she have left? Solution: def solution():

    return result

### Response: Question: A baker bakes 200 loaves of bread. He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread does he have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker bakes 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked / 2
    #He has
    loaves_left_after_morning = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning
    #loaves left after the morning.
    #He sells 1/2 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = loaves_left_after_morning / 2
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_left_after_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  Hotel Maid Nicole has to make 1000 cakes of soap.  She has a 55-gallon drum of soap base, which weighs 440 pounds.  How many ounces of fragrance and coloring does she need to add to the drum of soap base to make her 1000 cakes of soap? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #Hotel Maid Nicole has to make 1000 cakes of soap
    num_cakes = 1000
    #She has a 55-gallon drum of soap base, which weighs 440 pounds
    soap_base_weight = 440
    #A pound is 16 ounces
    pounds_to_ounces = 16
    #The total weight of the cakes of soap she wants to make is
    soap_cake_weight * num_cakes = 4 * 1000 = <<4*1000=4000>>4000
    #The total weight of the soap base is
    soap_base_weight * pounds_to_ounces = 440 * 16 = <<440*16=7040>>7040
    #The difference is
    result = 7040 - 4000 = <<7040-4000=3040>>3040
    return result

### Response: Question: A toy car can drive 20 miles on a full battery. The toy car's battery lasts for 2 hours. How many miles can the toy car drive in 4 hours? Solution: def solution():
    #The toy car can drive 20 miles on a full battery
    miles_per_battery = 20
    #The battery lasts for 2 hours
    hours_per_battery = 2
    #4 hours is 4/2 = <<4/2=2>>2 batteries
    num_batteries = 4 / hours_per_battery
    #The answer is
    result = miles_per_battery * num_batteries
    return result

### Response: Question: 20000 people live in a large town. 60% of the population are men. How many men live in the town? Solution: def solution():

    population = 20000
    #60% of the population are men
    men_percent = 60
    #40% of the population are women
    women_percent = 100 - men_percent
    #60% of the population are women
    men = population * men_percent / 100
    #The answer is
    result = men
    return result

### Response: Question: A gym can hold 200 people. The gym was 60% full. 100 more people came in. The gym was then 80% full. How many people can the gym hold? Solution: def solution():
    #The gym was 60% full
    gym_full_60 = 0.6
    #100 more people came in
    people_came_in = 100
    #The gym was then 80% full
    gym_full_80 = 0.8
    #The answer is
    result = (gym_full_80 - gym_full_60) * people_came_in
    return result

    #There were 12 patients

    monthly_cost = 10
    #If you pay for a year in advance the gym will give you two months free
    free_months = 2
    #A year is 12 months

    #The answer is

    #24 cans of soda cost $5

    return result

### Response: Question: A 100-liter tank has 50 liters of water. 10 liters of water are added to the tank each day. How many days will it take to fill the tank? Solution: def solution():
    #The tank has 50 liters of water
    water_initial = 50
    #10 liters of water are added each day
    water_added_per_day = 10
    #The tank is 100 liters
    water_tank_size = 100
    #The answer is
    result = (water_tank_size - water_initial) / water_added_per_day
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery sells 24 loaves of bread each day.  Monday through Friday, the bakery sells 24 loaves of bread.  On Saturday, the bakery sells 36 loaves of bread.  How many loaves of bread does the bakery sell in one week? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery sells 24 loaves of bread each day
    loaves_per_day = 24
    #Monday through Friday, the bakery sells 24 loaves of bread
    loaves_monday_friday = loaves_per_day * 5
    #On Saturday, the bakery sells 36 loaves of bread
    loaves_saturday = 36
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_monday_friday + loaves_saturday
    return result

### Response: Question: A 1000-page book has 200 pages of preface and 300 pages of appendices. How many pages of main content does it have? Solution: def solution():
    #The book has 200 pages of preface
    preface_pages = 200
    #and 300 pages of appendices
    appendix_pages = 300
    #The answer is
    result = 1000 - preface_pages - appendix_pages
    return result

### Response: Question: A warehouse has 2500 boxes. They receive 500 more boxes a day, from Monday to Thursday. How many boxes do they have now? Solution: def solution():
    #They have 2500 boxes
    boxes_initial = 2500
    #They receive 500 more boxes a day
    boxes_received_per_day = 500
    #There are 4 days between Monday and Thursday
    num_days = 4
    #They received
    boxes_received = boxes_received_per_day * num_days
    #The answer is
    result = boxes_initial + boxes_received
    return result

    return result

    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon

    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned

### Response: Question: The cafeteria has 200 plates. They wash 50 plates each hour, from 10:00 AM to 1:00 PM. How many plates do they have at 1:00 PM? Solution: def solution():
    #The cafeteria has 200 plates
    plates_initial = 200
    #They wash 50 plates an hour
    plates_washed_per_hour = 50
    #There are 3 hours between 10:00 AM and 1:00 PM
    num_hours = 3
    #They wash
    plates_washed = plates_washed_per_hour * num_hours
    #The answer is
    result = plates_initial - plates_washed
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery sells 100 loaves of bread on Monday. On Tuesday, it sells 50. On Wednesday, it sells 20. On Thursday, it sells 30. On Friday, it sells 40. How many loaves of bread did the bakery sell in a week? Solution: def solution
### Response: Question: A pizza place is selling pizzas for $12.  They have a $2 off coupon.  If you buy 2 pizzas, you get the 2nd pizza for half price.  How much do you pay for 2 pizzas with the coupon? Solution: def solution():
    #A pizza costs $12
    pizza_cost = 12
    #The coupon is for $2 off
    coupon_discount = 2
    #The second pizza is half price
    second_pizza_cost = pizza_cost / 2
    #The answer is
    result = pizza_cost + second_pizza_cost - coupon_discount
    return result

### Response: Question: The bakery has 200 loaves of bread. The bakery sells 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returns 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread does the bakery have left? Solution: def solution():

    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning = 93

    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is

### Response: Question: A 20-foot-long, 10-foot-wide, and 10-foot-tall box is filled with 1000 4-inch-long, 2-inch-wide, and 2-inch-tall boxes. How many 4-inch-long, 2-inch-wide, and 2-inch-tall boxes can fit in the 20-foot-long, 10-foot-wide, and 10-foot-tall box? Solution: def solution():
    #The large box is 20' long
    large_box_length = 20
    #The large box is 10' wide
    large_box_width = 10
    #The large box is 10' tall
    large_box_height = 10
    #The small box is 4" long
    small_box_length = 4
    #The small box is 2" wide
    small_box_width = 2
    #The small box is 2" tall
    small_box_height = 2
    #The large box is 20' long
    large_box_volume = large_box_length * large_box_width * large_box_height
    #The small box is 4" long
    small_box_volume = small_box_length * small_box_width * small_box_height
    #The answer is
    result = large_box_volume / small_box_volume
    return result

### Response: Question: A 20-pound bag of carrots has 120 carrots. A 20-pound bag of onions has 160 onions. A 20-pound bag of potatoes has 240 potatoes. A 20-pound bag of turnips has 280 turnips. What is the average number of vegetables in a 20-pound bag? Solution: def solution():
    #A 20-pound bag of carrots has 120 carrots
    carrots_per_bag = 120
    #A 20-pound bag of onions has 160 onions
    onions_per_bag = 160
    #A 20-pound bag of potatoes has 240 potatoes
    potatoes_per_bag = 240
    #A 20-pound bag of turnips has 280 turnips
    turnips_per_bag = 280
    #The total number of vegetables in 20-pound bags is
    total_vegetables = carrots_per_bag + onions_per_bag + potatoes_per_bag + turnips_per_bag
    #The number of 20-pound bags is
    num_bags = 4
    #The average number of vegetables in a 20-pound bag is
    result = total_vegetables / num_bags
    return result

### Response: Question: A 100-page book will take 4 hours to read at a rate of 25 pages per hour. How long will it take to read at a rate of 15 pages per hour? Solution: def solution():
    #A 100-page book will take 4 hours to read at a rate of 25 pages per hour
    book_length = 100
    pages_per_hour = 25
    hours_to_read = book_length / pages_per_hour
    #How long will it take to read at a rate of 15 pages per hour?
    pages_per_hour_slower = 15
    hours_to_read_slower = book_length / pages_per_hour_slower
    #The answer is
    result = hours_to_read_slower
    return result

    towels_lost = 20
    #The answer is
    result = towels_total - towels_washing - towels_drying - towels_lost
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery is making 2400 rolls. They have 4 ovens and each oven can bake 150 rolls at a time. How many times do they have to bake the rolls to make 2400? Solution: def solution():

    ovens = 4
    #Each oven can bake 150 rolls
    rolls_per_oven = 150
    #They need to bake 2400 rolls

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards. 6 of the players are midfielders. The rest of the players are defenders. How many players are defenders? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #6 are midfielders
    players_midfielders = 6
    #The rest are defenders
    players_defenders = players_total - players_forwards - players_midfielders
    return players_defenders

### Response: Question: The bakery made 200 donuts. They sold 93 donuts in the morning and 39 donuts in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 donuts. How many donuts did they have left? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: The 4th grade class is 2/3 the size of the 5th grade class.  The 5th grade class is 1/4 the size of the 6th grade class.  The 6th grade class has 24 students.  How many 4th graders are there? Solution: def solution():
    #The 6th grade class has 24 students
    sixth_grade_students = 24
    #The 5th grade class is 1/4 the size of the 6th grade class
    fifth_grade_students = sixth_grade_students / 4
    #The 4th grade class is 2/3 the size of the 5th grade class
    fourth_grade_students = fifth_grade_students * 2 / 3
    return fourth_grade_students

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces.  A bottle of detergent weighs 24 ounces.  A box of bleach weighs 12 ounces.  A bottle of fabric softener weighs 10 ounces.  A 10 pound bag of laundry weighs 160 ounces.  How many ounces of laundry supplies can you buy with a 10 pound bag of laundry? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake = 4
    #A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces
    soap_powder = 16
    #A bottle of detergent weighs 24 ounces
    detergent = 24
    #A box of bleach weighs 12 ounces
    bleach = 12
    #A bottle of fabric softener weighs 10 ounces
    fabric_softener = 10
    #A 10 pound bag of laundry weighs 160 ounces
    laundry = 160
    #The answer is
    result = laundry / (soap_cake + soap_powder + detergent + bleach + fabric_softener)
    return result

### Response: Question: A candy store sells 10000000 pieces of candy a day. On Tuesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy. On Wednesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy. On Thursday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy. On Friday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy. How many pieces of candy did it sell from Tuesday to Friday? Solution: def solution():
    #A candy store sells 10000000 pieces of candy a day
    candy_sold_per_day = 10000000
    #On Tuesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_tuesday = candy_sold_per_day
    #On Wednesday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_wednesday = candy_sold_per_day
    #On Thursday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_thursday = candy_sold_per_day
    #On Friday, it sold 10000000 pieces of candy
    candy_sold_friday = candy_sold_per_day
    #The answer is
    result = candy_sold_tuesday + candy_sold_wednesday + candy_sold_thursday + candy_sold_friday
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces. 2 cakes of soap are packaged together. A box of 48 soap cakes is shipped to a warehouse. What is the total weight, in ounces, of the box of soap cakes? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #2 cakes of soap are packaged together
    soap_package_weight = 2 * soap_cake_weight
    #A box of 48 soap cakes is shipped to a warehouse
    soap_cake_box_weight = 48 * soap_package_weight
    #The answer is
    result = soap_cake_box_weight
    return result

### Response: Question: The Beverly Hills Bakery baked 200 loaves of bread on Monday morning. They sold 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread did they have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakers started with 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning=93
    loaves_sold_afternoon=39
    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-pound box of oranges has 120 oranges. A 5-pound box of oranges has 60 oranges. How many oranges weigh one pound? Solution: def solution():
    #10 pounds of oranges is 120 oranges
    oranges_10_pounds = 120
    #5 pounds of oranges is 60 oranges
    oranges_5_pounds = 60
    #The difference is
    oranges_per_pound = (oranges_10_pounds - oranges_5_pounds) / 5
    return oranges_per_pound

### Response: Question: A bakery makes 200 loaves of bread a day. 40% of the bread is sold in the morning and 60% of the bread is sold in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread are not sold? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery makes 200 loaves of bread a day
    loaves_baked = 200
    #40% of the bread is sold in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked * 0.4
    #60% of the bread is sold in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = loaves_baked * 0.6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: A cafeteria in a high school sells 100 hamburgers every day. On Monday, they sold 10 hamburgers. On Tuesday, they sold 20 hamburgers. On Wednesday, they sold 15 hamburgers. On Thursday, they sold 25 hamburgers. On Friday, they sold 30 hamburgers. How many hamburgers did the cafeteria sell in the week? Solution: def solution():
    #The cafeteria sells 100 hamburgers a day
    hamburgers_per_day = 100
    #On Monday, they sold 10 hamburgers
    hamburgers_sold_monday = 10
    #On Tuesday, they sold 20 hamburgers
    hamburgers_sold_tuesday = 20
    #On Wednesday, they sold 15 hamburgers
    hamburgers_sold_wednesday = 15
    #On Thursday, they sold 25 hamburgers
    hamburgers_sold_thursday = 25
    #On Friday, they sold 30 hamburgers
    hamburgers_sold_friday = 30
    #The answer is
    result = hamburgers_sold_monday + hamburgers_sold_tuesday + hamburgers_sold_wednesday + hamburgers_sold_thursday + hamburgers_sold_friday
    return result

    second_customer_baguettes = 2
    second_customer_baguette_cost = 2
    second_customer_money = second_customer_baguettes * second_customer_baguette_cost
    #The third customer bought 1 croissant for $4
    third_customer_croissant_cost = 4
    third_customer_money = third_customer_croissant_cost
    #The fourth customer bought 1 muffin for $2
    fourth_customer_muffin_cost = 2
    fourth_customer_money = fourth_customer_muffin_cost
    #The answer is
    result = cashier_money_initial - first_customer_money - second_customer_money - third_customer_money - fourth_customer_money
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery has 12 cakes. The bakery sells 1/3 of the cakes in the morning and 2/3 of the cakes in the afternoon. How many cakes are left at the end of the day? Solution: def solution():

    #1/3 of the cakes are sold in the morning
    cakes_sold_morning = cakes_total / 3

    cakes_sold_afternoon = cakes_total / 3 * 2
    #The answer is

    return result

### Response: Question: 20000 liters of water are flowing through a pipe. 2000 liters of water are flowing into the pipe every minute. How many minutes will it take for the pipe to fill up? Solution: def solution():
    #The pipe has 20000 liters of water
    water_initial = 20000
    #2000 liters of water are flowing into the pipe every minute
    water_per_minute = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = water_initial / water_per_minute
    return result

### Response: Question: A 20-foot-long and 10-foot-wide room has 10-foot-high ceilings. What is the volume of the room? Solution: def solution():
    #The room is 20 feet long
    room_length = 20
    #The room is 10 feet wide
    room_width = 10
    #The room is 10 feet high
    room_height = 10
    #The answer is
    result = room_length * room_width * room_height
    return result

### Response: Question: The Beverly Hills Bakery baked 200 loaves of bread on Monday morning. They sold 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread did they have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakers started with 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning=93
    loaves_sold_afternoon=39
    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned
    return result

### Response: Question: A 12-pack of soda cans costs $4.00. A 24-pack of soda cans costs $7.00. How much money do you save by buying the 24-pack instead of 2 12-packs? Solution: def solution():

    soda_12_pack_cost = 4

### Response: Question: A 20-foot wall is to be built using 4-inch bricks. How many bricks are needed to build the wall? Solution: def solution():
    #A 20-foot wall is 20 * 12 = <<20*12=240>>240 inches
    wall_length = 240
    #A 4-inch brick is 4/12 = 1/3 of a foot
    brick_length = 1/3
    #240 inches / 4 inches = <<240/4=60>>60 bricks
    result = wall_length / brick_length
    return result

### Response: Question: The 20-member soccer team has 10 soccer balls. Each soccer ball is shared by 2 players. How many more soccer balls are needed so that each player has their own soccer ball? Solution: def solution():

    players = 20
    #Each ball is shared by 2 players
    players_per_ball = 2
    #The team has 10 soccer balls

    #The team needs 1 more soccer ball for each player
    soccer_balls_needed = players - soccer_balls
    #The answer is
    result = soccer_balls_needed
    return result

### Response: Question: The cafeteria has 200 chairs. 100 more chairs are added. 20 chairs are then removed. How many chairs are there now? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: A penguin is 2 feet tall.  A snake is 1/10 of the length of a penguin.  A giraffe is 100 times longer than a snake.  How tall is a giraffe? Solution: def solution():

    penguin_length = 2
    #A snake is 1/10 of the length of a penguin
    snake_length = penguin_length / 10
    #A giraffe is 100 times longer than a snake
    giraffe_length = snake_length * 100
    #The answer is
    result = giraffe_length

### Response: Question: A pizzaiolo is making pizzas. He has 12 pizzas in the oven. He can bake 4 pizzas at a time and it takes 15 minutes to bake each pizza. How long will it take to bake all 12 pizzas? Solution: def solution():
    #He can bake 4 pizzas at a time
    pizzas_per_batch = 4
    #It takes 15 minutes to bake a pizza
    minutes_per_pizza = 15
    #He has 12 pizzas
    pizzas_total = 12
    #He will need to bake
    num_batches = pizzas_total / pizzas_per_batch
    #batches of pizza. The answer is
    result = num_batches * minutes_per_pizza
    return result

### Response: Question: 10000000 people are in a theater. 1000000 people are in the orchestra section. 200000 people are in the balcony. How many people are on the main floor? Solution: def solution():
    #1000000 people are in the orchestra section
    orchestra_section = 1000000
    #200000 people are in the balcony
    balcony_section = 200000
    #The total number of people is
    total_people = orchestra_section + balcony_section
    #The answer is
    result = total_people - orchestra_section - balcony_section
    return result

### Response: Question: A 12-pack of soda cans costs $4.00. A 24-pack of soda cans costs $6.00. How much would it cost to buy 36 cans of soda? Solution: def solution():
    #12 cans of soda cost $4.00
    cost_12_cans = 4
    #24 cans of soda cost $6.00
    cost_24_cans = 6
    #36 cans of soda would cost
    cost_36_cans = (cost_12_cans * 3) / cost_24_cans
    return cost_36_cans

### Response: Question: A 12-pack of soda cans is on sale for $3.00.  The regular price is $3.75.  How much is the discount per can? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: 12 bakers baked 200 loaves of bread. 1/4 of the loaves were sold in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining loaves were sold in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread were not sold? Solution: def solution():
    #12 bakers baked 200 loaves of bread
    loaves_baked = 200
    #1/4 of the loaves were sold in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked / 4
    #1/2 of the remaining loaves were sold in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = (loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-foot-long and 12-foot-wide room is to be divided into two equal-sized rooms. What is the perimeter of each new room? Solution: def solution():
    #The original room is 10 feet long
    long_side = 10
    #and 12 feet wide
    short_side = 12
    #The perimeter of the original room is 2 * (long side) + 2 * (short side)
    perimeter_original = 2 * long_side + 2 * short_side
    #The new rooms are half the size, so the perimeter is
    perimeter_new = perimeter_original / 2
    return perimeter_new

### Response: Question: The gym has 200 towels. On Monday, 30 towels are washed. On Tuesday, 50 towels are washed. On Wednesday, 40 towels are washed. On Thursday, 20 towels are washed. On Friday, 30 towels are washed. How many towels are there at the end of Friday? Solution: def solution():
    #The gym started with 200 towels
    towels_initial = 200
    #On Monday, 30 towels were washed
    towels_washed_monday = 30
    #On Tuesday, 50 towels were washed
    towels_washed_tuesday = 50
    #On Wednesday, 40 towels were washed
    towels_washed_wednesday = 40
    #On Thursday, 20 towels were washed
    towels_washed_thursday = 20
    #On Friday, 30 towels were washed
    towels_washed_friday = 30
    #The answer is
    result = towels_initial - towels_washed_monday - towels_washed_tuesday - towels_washed_wednesday - towels_washed_thursday - towels_washed_friday
    return result

    #It sells 93 loaves

    #It has 7 loaves left at the end of the day

    return result

### Response: Question: The gym has 200 towels. On Monday, 32 towels are washed. On Tuesday, 58 towels are washed. On Wednesday, 26 towels are washed. On Thursday, 44 towels are washed. On Friday, 12 towels are washed. How many towels are left unwashed? Solution: def solution():
    #The gym started with 200 towels
    towels_initial = 200
    #On Monday, 32 towels were washed
    towels_washed_monday = 32
    #On Tuesday, 58 towels were washed
    towels_washed_tuesday = 58
    #On Wednesday, 26 towels were washed
    towels_washed_wednesday = 26
    #On Thursday, 44 towels were washed
    towels_washed_thursday = 44
    #On Friday, 12 towels were washed
    towels_washed_friday = 12
    #The total number of towels washed is
    towels_washed_total = towels_washed_monday + towels_washed_tuesday + towels_washed_wednesday + towels_washed_thursday + towels_washed_friday
    #The answer is
    result = towels_initial - towels_washed_total
    return result

### Response: Question: 123456789 is a 9-digit number. If you remove the last digit, the number is divisible by 9. What is the sum of all the digits in the number? Solution: def solution():
    #The number is 123456789
    number = 123456789
    #If you remove the last digit, the number is divisible by 9
    number_no_last_digit = number // 10
    #The sum of the digits is
    result = sum(int(digit) for digit in str(number_no_last_digit))
    return result

    #The 2020 census found 20% more people
    people_2020_increase = 0.2
    #The answer is
    result = people_2010 * (1 + people_2020_increase) - people

    players_usa = 15
    #6 of the players are from Mexico

    return result

### Response: Question: 1200 people are at a soccer game. 1/2 of the people are from the home team and 1/4 of the people are from the away team. How many people are there who are not part of either team? Solution: def solution():
    #1200 people are at a soccer game
    people_total = 1200
    #1/2 of the people are from the home team
    people_home = people_total / 2
    #1/4 of the people are from the away team
    people_away = people_total / 4
    #The answer is
    result = people_total - people_home - people_away
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake bakery can bake 100 cakes a day. It is open 7 days a week. How many cakes can it b
### Response: Question: The sushi restaurant sells 20 rolls on Monday, 30 rolls on Tuesday, and 25 rolls on Wednesday. How many sushi rolls did they sell in total? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: A 12-pack of soda costs $3. A 24-pack of soda costs $5. How much would it cost to buy 36 cans of soda? Solution: def solution():
    #A 12-pack of soda costs $3
    soda_12_pack_cost = 3
    #A 24-pack of soda costs $5
    soda_24_pack_cost = 5
    #36 cans of soda would be
    soda_36_pack_size = 36
    #3 12-packs of soda
    soda_12_packs_needed = soda_36_pack_size / 12
    #3 12-packs of soda would cost
    soda_12_packs_cost = soda_12_pack_cost * soda_12_packs_needed
    #2 24-packs of soda
    soda_24_packs_needed = (soda_36_pack_size - soda_12_packs_needed * 12) / 24
    #2 24-packs of soda would cost
    soda_24_packs_cost = soda_24_packs_needed * soda_24_pack_cost
    #The answer is
    result = soda_12_packs_cost + soda_24_packs_cost
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery has 1200 cookies. They have 100 customers. Each customer can buy a maximum of 12 cookies. How many customers will be turned away because there are not enough cookies? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery has 1200 cookies
    cookies_initial = 1200
    #They have 100 customers
    customers = 100
    #Each customer can buy 12 cookies
    cookies_per_customer = 12
    #The answer is
    result = customers - (cookies_initial // cookies_per_customer)
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-foot by 10-foot room has 200 square feet of floor space. How many 12-inch by 12-inch tiles will it take to cover the floor? Solution: def solution():
    #The room is 10 feet by 10 feet
    room_length = 10
    room_width = 10
    #200 square feet of floor space
    floor_space = 200
    #12 inches is 1 foot
    tile_length = 12
    tile_width = 12
    #The answer is
    result = floor_space / (tile_length * tile_width)
    return result

### Response: Question: A baker bakes 200 loaves of bread a day. He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning and 1/2 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread does he have left at the end of the day? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker bakes 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked / 2
    #He sells 1/2 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = (loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning) / 2
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: A catering company is catering a party. 50 people are coming to the party. 20 of the guests are vegetarians. 10 of the guests are vegans. 30 of the guests are omnivores. The catering company has to provide 2000 calories to each omnivore, 1500 calories to each vegetarian, and 1000 calories to each vegan. How many calories of food does the catering company need to provide? Solution: def solution():
    #There are 50 people at the party
    party_guests = 50
    #20 of the guests are vegetarians
    vegetarians = 20
    #10 of the guests are vegans
    vegans = 10
    #30 of the guests are omnivores
    omnivores = 30
    #The vegetarians need 1500 calories each
    vegetarian_calories = 1500
    #The vegans need 1000 calories each
    vegan_calories = 1000
    #The omnivores need 2000 calories each
    omnivore_calories = 2000
    #The answer is
    result = (vegetarians * vegetarian_calories) + (vegans * vegan_calories) + (omnivores * omnivore_calories)
    return result

### Response: Question: 35000 people live in a city. 5000 more people move in. 1000 people move out. How many people are left? Solution: def solution():

    people_initial = 35000
    #5000 more people move in
    people_moved_in = 5000
    #1000 people move out
    people_moved_out = 1000
    #The answer is

    return result

### Response: Question: The 7th grade soccer team has 15 players. 1/3 of the players are from the 8th grade. 2/3 of the 8th graders are boys. How many boys from the 8th grade are on the soccer team? Solution: def solution():
    #The soccer team has 15 players
    players = 15
    #1/3 of the players are from the 8th grade
    ighth_grade_players = players / 3
    #2/3 of the 8th graders are boys

    #The answer is

    return result
### Response: Question: The pizza place has a 2 for 1 deal on pizza.  If a pizza costs $12, how much would it cost to buy 4 pizzas? Solution: def solution():
    #The pizza place has a 2 for 1 deal on pizza.  If a pizza costs $12, how much would it cost to buy 4 pizzas?
    pizza_cost = 12
    pizzas_bought = 4
    pizzas_free = pizzas_bought / 2
    pizzas_paid = pizzas_bought - pizzas_free
    result = pizza_cost * pizzas_paid
    return result

### Response: Question: A pizza parlor sells pizzas for $10 each.  They also sell a "Meal Deal" which includes 2 pizzas and 2 orders of breadsticks for $25.  How much money do you save, per pizza, by buying the Meal Deal? Solution: def solution():
    #The Meal Deal costs $25
    meal_deal_cost = 25
    #The Meal Deal includes 2 pizzas
    meal_deal_pizzas = 2
    #The Meal Deal includes 2 orders of breadsticks
    meal_deal_breadsticks = 2
    #The pizzas are $10 each
    pizza_cost = 10
    #The breadsticks are $5 each
    breadstick_cost = 5
    #The cost of the pizzas in the Meal Deal is
    meal_deal_pizza_cost = meal_deal_pizzas * pizza_cost
    #The cost of the breadsticks in the Meal Deal is
    meal_deal_breadstick_cost = meal_deal_breadsticks * breadstick_cost
    #The cost of the Meal Deal without the pizzas is
    meal_deal_cost_without_pizzas = meal_deal_cost - meal_deal_pizza_cost
    #The cost of the Meal Deal without the breadsticks is
    meal_deal_cost_without_breadsticks = meal_deal_cost - meal_deal_breadstick_cost

### Response: Question: A sack of oranges weighs 40 pounds. A sack of onions weighs 20 pounds. A sack of potatoes weighs 50 pounds. A sack of radishes weighs 10 pounds. A sack of strawberries weighs 15 pounds. A sack of turnips weighs 30 pounds. A sack of zucchini weighs 25 pounds. A truck can carry 10 sacks. How many pounds of vegetables can a truck carry? Solution: def solution():
    #A sack of oranges weighs 40 pounds
    oranges_weight = 40
    #A sack of onions weighs 20 pounds
    onions_weight = 20
    #A sack of potatoes weighs 50 pounds
    potatoes_weight = 50
    #A sack of radishes weighs 10 pounds
    radishes_weight = 10
    #A sack of strawberries weighs 15 pounds
    strawberries_weight = 15
    #A sack of turnips weighs 30 pounds
    turnips_weight = 30
    #A sack of zucchini weighs 25 pounds
    zucchini_weight = 25
    #A truck can carry 10 sacks
    truck_capacity = 10
    #The answer is
    result = oranges_weight + onions_weight + potatoes_weight + radishes_weight + strawberries_weight + turnips_weight + zucchini_weight * truck_capacity

### Response: Question: A 12-hour clock is made up of 60 minutes. How many minutes is the 18-hour clock made up of? Solution: def solution():
    #The 12-hour clock is made up of 60 minutes
    minutes_in_12_hour_clock = 60
    #The 18-hour clock is 12/18 = <<12/18=2/3>>2/3 times bigger
    minutes_in_18_hour_clock = minutes_in_12_hour_clock * (2/3)
    #The answer is
    result = minutes_in_18_hour_clock
    return result

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards, and 8 of the players are midfielders. The rest of the players are defenders. How many defenders are there? Solution: def solution():
    #A soccer team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 of the players are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #8 of the players are midfielders
    players_midfielders = 8
    #The rest of the players are defenders. The answer is
    result = players_total - players_forwards - players_midfielders
    return result

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are from the United States. 6 of the players are from Brazil. 2 of the players are from Spain. 4 of the players are from England. How many players are not from these 4 countries? Solution: def solution():

    players = 24
    #12 are from the US
    players_US = 12
    #6 are from Brazil
    players_Brazil = 6
    #2 are from Spain
    players_Spain = 2
    #4 are from England
    players_England = 4
    #The answer is

    return result

### Response: Question: The bakers at the Beverly Hills Bakery baked 200 loaves of bread on Monday morning. They sold 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread did they have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakers started with 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning=93
    loaves_sold_afternoon=39
    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery is making 120 loaves of bread. They have 10 bakers who can bake 12 loaves of bread each. How many more bakers do they need? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery has 10 bakers
    bakers_initial = 10
    #Each baker can bake 12 loaves
    loaves_per_baker = 12
    #They need to bake 120 loaves
    loaves_needed = 120
    #They can bake with their current staff
    loaves_current = bakers_initial * loaves_per_baker
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_needed - loaves_current
    return result

### Response: Question: The gym was selling 1-year memberships for $300 and 3-year memberships for $750. 20 people bought 1-year memberships and 10 people bought 3-year memberships. How much money did the gym make? Solution: def solution():
    #1 year membership is $300
    one_year_membership = 300
    #3 year membership is $750
    three_year_membership = 750
    #20 people bought 1 year memberships
    one_year_members = 20
    #10 people bought 3 year memberships
    three_year_members = 10
    #The gym made 20 * $300 = $<<20*300=600>>600 from 1 year memberships
    one_year_membership_revenue = one_year_members * one_year_membership
    #The gym made 10 * $750 = $<<10*750=7500>>7500 from 3 year memberships
    three_year_membership_revenue = three_year_members * three_year_membership
    #The gym made $600 + $7500 = $<<600+7500=8100>>8100
    result = one_year_membership_revenue + three_year_membership_revenue
    return result

### Response: Question: A sack of flour weighs 50 pounds. A sack of sugar weighs 40 pounds. A sack of salt weighs 30 pounds. A sack of baking powder weighs 20 pounds. A sack of yeast weighs 10 pounds. A bakery van can carry a maximum weight of 2000 pounds. How many sacks of yeast can the bakery van carry along with 2 sacks each of flour, sugar, salt and baking powder? Solution: def solution():
    #A sack of flour weighs 50 pounds
    flour_weight = 50
    #A sack of sugar weighs 40 pounds
    sugar_weight = 40
    #A sack of salt weighs 30 pounds
    salt_weight = 30
    #A sack of baking powder weighs 20 pounds
    baking_powder_weight = 20
    #A sack of yeast weighs 10 pounds
    yeast_weight = 10
    #A bakery van can carry a maximum weight of 2000 pounds
    van_weight_limit = 2000
    #2 sacks each of flour, sugar, salt and baking powder weigh
    flour_sugar_salt_baking_powder_weight = 2 * (flour_weight + sugar_weight + salt_weight + baking_powder_weight)
    #The answer is
    result = van_weight_limit - flour_sugar_salt_baking_powder_weight
    return result

### Response: Question: The soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are from the United States, 6 are from Mexico, and the rest are from Canada. How many players are from Canada? Solution: def solution():

    #6 are from Mexico
    players_mexico = 6
    #The rest are from Canada

    return players_canada

    #She will be 18 in 18-12=<<18-12=6>>6 years
    years_to_18 = 6

    #She will grow 2*6=<<2*6=12>>12 inches

### Response: Question: A 12-pack of soda cans is on sale for $3.00. A 24-pack of soda cans is on sale for $5.00. How much money do you save by buying the 24-pack of soda cans? Solution: def solution():
    #12 cans of soda are on sale for $3.00
    cans_12 = 12
    dollars_12 = 3
    #24 cans of soda are on sale for $5.00
    cans_24 = 24
    dollars_24 = 5
    #The 12-pack costs $3.00 / 12 cans = $<<3/12=0.25>>0.25 per can
    cost_per_can_12 = dollars_12 / cans_12
    #The 24-pack costs $5.00 / 24 cans = $<<5/24=0.20833333333333332>>0.20833333333333332 per can
    cost_per_can_24 = dollars_24 / cans_24
    #The 24-pack is cheaper, so the savings is 0.25 - 0.20833333333333332 =
    savings = cost_per_can_12 - cost_per_can_24
    #The answer is
    result = savings * cans_24
    return result

### Response: Question: 12000 people attended the soccer game. 75% of the attendees were men. How many women attended the soccer game? Solution: def solution():
    #12000 people attended the soccer game
    attendees = 12000
    #75% of the attendees were men
    men_percent = 0.75
    #The number of men is
    men = attendees * men_percent
    #The number of women is
    women = attendees - men
    #The answer is
    result = women
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-foot by 10-foot room has 200 square feet of floor space. How many 12-inch by 12-inch tiles will it take to cover the floor? Solution: def solution():
    #The room is 10 feet by 10 feet
    room_length = 10
    room_width = 10
    #The room has 200 square feet of floor space
    floor_space = 200
    #12 inches is 1 foot
    tile_length = 12
    tile_width = 12
    #The number of tiles is
    tiles = floor_space / (tile_length * tile_width)
    return tiles
Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write
### Response: Question: The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of April was 2.5 inches.  The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of May was 4.5 inches.  The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of June was 3.5 inches.  The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of July was 2.0 inches.  What is the average amount of rainfall for these 4 months? Solution: def solution():
    #The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of April was 2.5 inches.
    april_rainfall = 2.5
    #The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of May was 4.5 inches.
    may_rainfall = 4.5
    #The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of June was 3.5 inches.
    june_rainfall = 3.5
    #The 30-day total for the amount of rainfall in the month of July was 2.0 inches.
    july_rainfall = 2.0
    #The total rainfall for the 4 months is
    total_rainfall = april_rainfall + may_rainfall + june_rainfall + july_rainfall
    #The average rainfall is
    result = total_rainfall / 4
    return result

    return result

### Response: Question: A baker is making a 3-layer cake. The first layer is 10 inches in diameter. The second layer is 8 inches in diameter. The third layer is 6 inches in diameter. What is the total volume of the cake? Solution: def solution():
    #The first layer is 10 inches in diameter
    layer_1_diameter = 10
    #The second layer is 8 inches in diameter
    layer_2_diameter = 8
    #The third layer is 6 inches in diameter
    layer_3_diameter = 6
    #The height of the cake is 4 inches
    cake_height = 4
    #The volume of a cylinder is pi * radius^2 * height
    #The first layer has a radius of 10/2 = <<10/2=5>>5 inches
    layer_1_radius = 5
    layer_1_volume = 3.14 * (layer_1_radius)**2 * cake_height
    #The second layer has a radius of 8/2 = <<8/2=4>>4 inches
    layer_2_radius = 4
    layer_2_volume = 3.14 * (layer_2_radius)**2 * cake_height
    #The third layer has a radius of 6/2 = <<6/2=3>>3 inches
    layer_3_radius = 3
    layer_3_volume = 3.14 * (layer_3_radius)**2 * cake_height
    #The total volume is
    result = layer_1_volume + layer_2_volume + layer_3_volume
    return result

### Response: Question: A candy shop sells lollipops, gummy bears, and sour worms. The lollipops cost $1.50 each, the gummy bears cost $2.50 each, and the sour worms cost $3.50 each. On Tuesday, the candy shop sold 10 lollipops, 15 gummy bears, and 5 sour worms. How much money did the candy shop make on Tuesday? Solution: def solution():
    #The lollipops cost $1.50 each
    lollipop_cost = 1.5
    #The gummy bears cost $2.50 each
    gummy_bear_cost = 2.5
    #The sour worms cost $3.50 each
    sour_worm_cost = 3.5
    #10 lollipops at $1.50 each cost
    lollipop_revenue = lollipop_cost * 10
    #15 gummy bears at $2.50 each cost
    gummy_bear_revenue = gummy_bear_cost * 15
    #5 sour worms at $3.50 each cost
    sour_worm_revenue = sour_worm_cost * 5
    #The answer is
    result = lollipop_revenue + gummy_bear_revenue + sour_worm_revenue
    return result

### Response: Question: 10000000 people are in a theater. 1/4 of the audience is children. 1/2 of the adults are men. How many women are in the audience? Solution: def solution():
    #10000000 people are in a theater
    people_initial = 10000000
    #1/4 of the audience is children
    children_fraction = 1/4
    #1/2 of the adults are men
    men_fraction = 1/2
    #The answer is
    result = people_initial - (people_initial * children_fraction) - (people_initial * men_fraction)
    return result

### Response: Question: 3524264 is the 4-digit number with the second-highest sum of digits. What is the highest 4-digit number with the sum of digits? Solution: def solution():
    #3524264 is the 4-digit number with the second-highest sum of digits
    number_second_highest = 3524264
    #The sum of the digits of a number is
    def sum_digits(number):
        return number.sum()
    #The highest 4-digit number with the sum of digits is
    result = max(range(1000, 10000), key=sum_digits)
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces.  A bottle of liquid soap weighs 12 ounces.  A customer at the grocery store has 2 cakes of soap, 3 boxes of soap powder, and 1 bottle of liquid soap.  How much do the customer' -s purchases weigh? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #A box of soap powder weighs 16 ounces
    soap_powder_weight = 16
    #A bottle of liquid soap weighs 12 ounces
    liquid_soap_weight = 12
    #The customer has 2 cakes of soap
    soap_cakes = 2
    #3 boxes of soap powder
    soap_powder_boxes = 3
    #and 1 bottle of liquid soap
    liquid_soap_bottles = 1
    #The cakes of soap weigh
    soap_cake_total_weight = soap_cakes * soap_cake_weight
    #The boxes of soap powder weigh
    soap_powder_total_weight = soap_powder_boxes * soap_powder_weight
    #The bottles of liquid soap weigh
    liquid_soap_total_weight = liquid_soap_bottles * liquid_soap_weight
    #The answer is
    result = soap_cake_total_weight + soap_powder_total_weight + liquid_soap_total_weight
    return result

    result = 2
    return result

### Response: Question: 10000000 people are in a theater. 1000000 of them are children. The rest are adults. Each child's ticket cost $3. Each adult's ticket cost $4. How much money did the theater make? Solution: def solution():
    #1000000 out of 10000000 are children
    children_percent = 0.1
    #The rest are adults
    adults_percent = 1 - children_percent
    #The theater sold 10000000 * children_percent = <<1000000=1000000>>1000000 children's tickets
    children_tickets = 10000000 * children_percent
    #The theater sold 10000000 * adults_percent = <<10000000*0.9=9000000>>9000000 adult tickets
    adult_tickets = 10000000 * adults_percent
    #The theater made 1000000 * 3 = <<1000000*3=3000000>>3000000 from children's tickets
    children_ticket_revenue = children_tickets * 3
    #The theater made 9000000 * 4 = <<9000000*4=36000000>>36000000 from adult tickets
    adult_ticket_revenue = adult_tick

### Response: Question: A baker is making a cake. The cake recipe calls for 2.5 cups of flour, 1.5 cups of sugar, 0.25 cups of baking soda, and 1 cup of milk. The baker has 5.5 cups of flour, 4.5 cups of sugar, 1.5 cups of baking soda, and 2 cups of milk. Does the baker have enough ingredients to make the cake? Solution: def solution():
    #The cake needs 2.5 cups of flour
    flour_needed = 2.5
    #The baker has 5.5 cups of flour
    flour_available = 5.5
    #The cake needs 1.5 cups of sugar
    sugar_needed = 1.5
    #The baker has 4.5 cups of sugar
    sugar_available = 4.5
    #The cake needs 0.25 cups of baking soda
    baking_soda_needed = 0.25
    #The baker has 1.5 cups of baking soda
    baking_soda_available = 1.5
    #The cake needs 1 cup of milk
    milk_needed = 1
    #The baker has 2 cups of milk
    milk_available = 2
    #The answer is
    result = flour_available >= flour_needed and sugar_available >= sugar_needed and baking_soda_available >= baking_soda_needed and milk_available >= milk_needed
    return result

### Response: Question: 2000000 people are in a theater. 1000000 of them are adults. The rest are children. Each adult has 2 children with them. How many children are in the theater? Solution: def solution():
    #1000000 of the 2000000 people are adults
    adults = 1000000
    #The rest are children
    children = 2000000 - adults
    #Each adult has 2 children with them
    children_per_adult = 2
    #The answer is
    result = children + (adults * children_per_adult)
    return result

### Response: Question: In 100-meter races, the current world record is 9.58 seconds. The second-fastest time is 9.69 seconds. The third-fastest time is 9.72 seconds. How many tenths of a second faster is the world record than the third-fastest time? Solution: def solution():
    #The world record is 9.58 seconds
    world_record = 9.58
    #The third fastest time is 9.72 seconds
    third_fastest = 9.72
    #The difference is
    difference = world_record - third_fastest
    #The answer is
    result = difference * 10
    return result

### Response: Question: A baker has 100 loaves of bread. He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning and 1/3 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread does he have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker has 100 loaves
    loaves = 100
    #He sells 1/2 of the loaves in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves / 2
    #He has
    loaves_remaining = loaves - loaves_sold_morning
    #loaves remaining.
    #He sells 1/3 of the remaining loaves in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = loaves_remaining / 3
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_remaining - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: The Beverly Hills Bakery baked 200 loaves of bread on Monday morning. They sold 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread did they have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakers started with 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning=93
    loaves_sold_afternoon=39
    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned
    return result

### Response: Question: The cafeteria at the University of Texas at Austin serves 25,000 students. 20% of the students are on the meal plan. How many students are not on the meal plan? Solution: def solution():
    #20% of the students are on the meal plan
    meal_plan_percent = 0.2
    #25,000 students are served
    students_served = 25000
    #The answer is
    result = students_served * (1 - meal_plan_percent)
    return result

    return result

### Response: Question: The cafeteria has 120 students. 40% of the students have pizza, 20% of the students have a hamburger, and the rest have a salad. How many students are eating a salad? Solution: def solution():
    #The cafeteria has 120 students
    students = 120
    #40% of the students have pizza
    pizza_students = students * 0.4
    #20% of the students have a hamburger
    hamburger_students = students * 0.2
    #The rest have a salad
    salad_students = students - pizza_students - hamburger_students

### Response: Question: A catering company is hired to cater a 3-day event.  They are to provide 2000 meals each day.  The first day they have 10 servers and each server can serve 20 meals.  The second day they have 15 servers and each server can serve 25 meals.  The third day they have 12 servers and each server can serve 30 meals.  How many servers are needed to serve the full 3 days? Solution: def solution():
    #The catering company is to provide 2000 meals each day
    meals_per_day = 2000
    #The first day they have 10 servers and each server can serve 20 meals
    servers_day_1 = 10
    meals_per_server_day_1 = 20
    #The second day they have 15 servers and each server can serve 25 meals
    servers_day_2 = 15
    meals_per_server_day_2 = 25
    #The third day they have 12 servers and each server can serve 30 meals
    servers_day_3 = 12
    meals_per_server_day_3 = 30
    #The answer is
    result = meals_per_day / meals_per_server_day_1 + meals_per_day / meals_per_server_day_2 + meals_per_day / meals_per_server_day_3
    return result

### Response: Question: A baker is making a cake. The cake recipe calls for 3 cups of flour, 1.5 cups of sugar, and 1/2 a cup of butter. The baker has 10 cups of flour, 4.5 cups of sugar, and 1.5 cups of butter. How many cakes can the baker make? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker has 10 cups of flour
    flour = 10
    #The baker has 4.5 cups of sugar
    sugar = 4.5
    #The baker has 1.5 cups of butter
    butter = 1.5
    #The cake recipe calls for 3 cups of flour
    flour_per_cake = 3
    #The cake recipe calls for 1.5 cups of sugar
    sugar_per_cake = 1.5
    #The cake recipe calls for 1/2 a cup of butter
    butter_per_cake = 0.5
    #The baker has enough flour to make
    flour_cakes = flour / flour_per_cake
    #The baker has enough sugar to make
    sugar_cakes = sugar / sugar_per_cake
    #The baker has enough butter to make
    butter_cakes = butter / butter_per_cake
    #The baker can make
    result = min(flour_cakes, sugar_cakes, butter_cakes)
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-ounce soda has 6 ounces of sugar. How many ounces of sugar are in a 12-pack of soda? Solution: def solution():
    #A 10-ounce soda has 6 ounces of sugar
    soda_size = 10
    soda_sugar = 6
    #A 12-pack of soda has 12 * 10 = <<12*10=120>>120 ounces of soda
    twelve_pack_soda = 12 * soda_size
    #The answer is
    result = twelve_pack_soda * soda_sugar / soda_size
### Response: Question: A 10-foot-long and 12-foot-wide room is to be divided into two equal-sized rooms. How many square feet is the smaller room? Solution: def solution():
    #The original room is 10 feet long
    long_side = 10
    #and 12 feet wide
    short_side = 12
    #To find the area, we use the formula
    area_formula = long_side * short_side
    #The area of the original room is
    area_original = area_formula
    #To divide the room in half, we divide the area by 2
    area_half = area_original / 2
    #The answer is
    result = area_half
    return result

### Response: Question: A 10-foot-long, 12-foot-wide, and 8-foot-high box is 4/5 full of apples. How many apples are in the box? Solution: def solution():

    box_width = 12
    #The box is 8 feet high
    box_height = 8
    #The box is 4/5 full of apples
    box_fullness = 4/5
    #The answer is
    result = box_length * box_width * box_height * box_fullness
    return result

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards, and the rest are goalkeepers and defenders. There are 2 goalkeepers. How many defenders are there? Solution: def solution():

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 1/3 of the players are from the United States, and 1/5 of the players are from Brazil. How many players are from the United States and Brazil? Solution: def solution():

    players = 24
    #1/3 of the players are from the United States

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. The team is divided into 3 groups of 8 players. Each group has 2 goalies. How many non-goalies are there? Solution: def solution():
    #The team has 3 groups of 8 players
    players_per_group = 8
    #There are 2 goalies in each group
    goalies_per_group = 2
    #The team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #The number of non-goalies is
    result = players_total - (players_per_group * goalies_per_group)
    return result

    #300000 of them are wearing blue
    blue = 300000
    #The rest are wearing yellow

    return yellow

### Response: Question: A 20-foot-long and 10-foot-wide room has 4 windows. Each window is 2 feet wide. What is the total area of the walls? Solution: def solution():
    #The room is 20 feet long
    length = 20
    #The room is 10 feet wide
    width = 10
    #The room has 4 windows
    num_windows = 4
    #Each window is 2 feet wide
    window_width = 2
    #The total window space is
    window_space = num_windows * window_width
    #The room's total wall space is
    wall_space = 2 * (length + width) - window_space
    return wall_space

### Response: Question: 36000 gallons of water are flowing into a reservoir at a rate of 400 gallons per minute. The reservoir can hold 48000 gallons of water. How many minutes will it take to fill the reservoir? Solution: def solution():
    #The reservoir is filling at 400 gallons per minute
    gallons_per_minute = 400
    #The reservoir can hold 48000 gallons
    gallons_max = 48000
    #The reservoir is currently 36000 gallons full
    gallons_initial = 36000
    #The reservoir needs to fill
    gallons_needed = gallons_max - gallons_initial
    #The answer is
    result = gallons_needed / gallons_per_minute
    return result

### Response: Question: The bakery bakes 100 loaves of bread a day. 40% of the loaves are sold in the morning and 60% of the loaves are sold in the afternoon. How many loaves of bread are not sold? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery bakes 100 loaves of bread a day
    loaves_baked = 100
    #40% of the loaves are sold in the morning
    loaves_sold_morning = loaves_baked * 0.4
    #60% of the loaves are sold in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_afternoon = loaves_baked * 0.6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon
    return result

### Response: Question: The cafeteria has 300 students and 50 staff. 10% of the students and 20% of the staff buy a soda each day. How many sodas are sold per day? Solution: def solution():
    #The cafeteria has 300 students
    students = 300
    #And 50 staff
    staff = 50
    #10% of the students buy a soda
    students_sodas = students * 0.1
    #And 20% of the staff buy a soda
    staff_sodas = staff * 0.2
    #The answer is
    result = students_sodas + staff_sodas
    return result

    height_growth = 6
    #In 10 years, the child will have grown

    return result

### Response: Question: 200 people were in the audience at a theater. If each person in the audience applauds 5 times, what is
### Response: Question: A bakery bakes 200 loaves of bread. 93 loaves are sold in the morning and 39 loaves are sold in the afternoon. A grocery store returns 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread does the bakery have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery started with 200 loaves
    loaves_baked = 200
    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning = 93
    loaves_sold_afternoon = 39
    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_baked - loaves_sold_morning - loaves_sold_afternoon + loaves_returned
    return result

### Response: Question: The 100-yard dash is a sprinting race.  The current record is 9.58 seconds.  Usain Bolt is the fastest runner in the world.  He can run the 100-yard dash in 9.6 seconds.  How much faster is Bolt than the average runner? Solution: def solution():
    #The current record is 9.58 seconds
    record = 9.58
    #Usain Bolt can run it in 9.6 seconds
    bolt = 9.6
    #The answer is
    result = record - bolt
    return result

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces. 12 cakes of soap are packed in each box. How many ounces of soap are in 3 boxes? Solution: def solution():

    #12 cakes of soap are packed in each box

### Response: Question: A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces.  Hotel Maidstone orders soap in boxes of 108 cakes.  How many ounces of soap does Hotel Maidstone receive when they order 2 boxes? Solution: def solution():
    #A cake of soap weighs 4 ounces
    soap_cake_weight = 4
    #Hotel Maidstone orders boxes of 108 cakes
    soap_cake_box = 108
    #When they order 2 boxes, the weight of the soap in ounces is
    soap_weight = soap_cake_weight * soap_cake_box * 2
    return soap_weight

### Response: Question: Olivia has $23. She bought five bagels for $3 each. How much money does she have left? Solution: def solution():
    #Olivia started with $23
    money_initial = 23
    #She bought 5 bagels
    bagels = 5
    #Each bagel cost $3
    bagel_cost = 3
    #5 bagels at $3 a bagel cost
    money_spent = bagels * bagel_cost
    #The answer is
    result = money_initial - money_spent

### Response: Question: A 10-year-old boy is 4 feet 3 inches tall.  How tall will he be in 12 years if he grows 6 inches per year? Solution: def solution():
    #The boy is 4 feet 3 inches tall
    feet_initial = 4
    inches_initial = 3
    #He will grow 6 inches per year
    inches_grown_per_year = 6
    #In 12 years, he will grow
    inches_grown_total = inches_grown_per_year * 12
    #The answer is
    result = feet_initial * 12 + inches_initial + inches_grown_total
    return result

### Response: Question: The 4th grade class is on a field trip. The class has 26 students and 2 teachers. 1/3 of the students are boys. How many girls are on the field trip? Solution: def solution():
    #The class has 26 students
    students = 26
    #1/3 of the students are boys
    boys = 1/3 * students
    #The answer is
    result = students - boys
### Response: Question: A 10-foot-long and 12-foot-wide rectangular room is to be divided into two equal-sized rooms. How many feet is the perimeter of one of the new rooms? Solution: def solution():
    #The original room is 10 feet long
    long_side = 10
    #and 12 feet wide
    short_side = 12
    #The perimeter of the original room is 2 * long side + 2 * short side
    perimeter_original = 2 * long_side + 2 * short_side
    #The perimeter of one of the new rooms is half the perimeter of the original room
    perimeter_new = perimeter_original

### Response: Question: A 24-pack of soda cans is on sale for $5.00. A 24-pack of beer cans is on sale for $12.00. How much more do the beer cans cost per can than the soda cans? Solution: def solution():
    #24 cans of soda cost $5.00
    soda_cost = 5.00
    #24 cans of beer cost $12.00
    beer_cost = 12.00
    #The answer is
    result = (beer_cost - soda_cost) / 24
    return result

### Response: Question: A 24-pack of soda cans costs $12.00.  A 12-pack of soda cans costs $6.00.  How much would it cost to buy 48 cans of soda? Solution: def solution():
    #A 24-pack of soda cans costs $12.00
    soda_24_pack_cost = 12.00
    #A 12-pack of soda cans costs $6.00
    soda_12_pack_cost = 6.00
    #48 cans of soda would be 2 * 24 cans
    soda_24_packs_needed = 48 / 24
    #24 packs of soda would cost
    soda_24_packs_cost = soda_24_pack_cost * soda_24_packs_needed
    #48 cans of soda would be 4 * 12 cans
    soda_12_packs_needed = 48 / 12
    #12 packs of soda would cost
    soda_12_packs_cost = soda_12_pack_cost * soda_12_packs_needed
    #The answer is
    result = soda_24_packs_cost + soda_12_packs_cost
    return result

### Response: Question: The pizza parlor has a special on 4-slice pizzas.  If you buy 10 4-slice pizzas, you get 20% off.  How much would it cost to buy 10 4-slice pizzas? Solution: def solution():
    #The pizza parlor has a special on 4-slice pizzas.  If you buy 10 4-slice pizzas, you get 20% off.  How much would it cost to buy 10 4-slice pizzas?
    pizza_slices = 4
    pizzas_bought = 10
    pizza_discount = 0.2
    pizza_price = 4
    pizzas_bought_discounted = pizzas_bought * (1 - pizza_discount)
    pizzas_bought_undiscounted = pizzas_bought * (1 + pizza_discount)
    pizza_cost = pizza_price * pizza_slices
    pizzas_bought_cost = pizzas_bought * pizza_cost
    pizzas_bought_discounted_cost = pizzas_bought_discounted * pizza_cost
    pizzas_bought_undiscounted_cost = pizzas_bought_undiscounted * pizza_cost
    result = pizzas_bought_discounted_cost
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery sells 200 loaves of bread on Monday. They sell 50 more loaves of bread on Tuesday. On Wednesday, they sell 100 less loaves of bread than on Tuesday. How many loaves of bread did they sell on Wednesday? Solution: def solution():

    loaves_monday = 200
    #On Tuesday, they sold 50 more loaves
    loaves_tuesday = loaves_monday + 50
    #On Wednesday, they sold 100 less loaves than on Tuesday
    loaves_wednesday = loaves_tuesday - 100
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_wednesday
    return result

### Response: Question: A sack of onions weighs 50 pounds. A sack of carrots weighs 20 pounds. A sack of potatoes weighs 30 pounds. A sack of cabbages weighs 40 pounds. A sack of radishes weighs 10 pounds. A sack of beets weighs 15 pounds. How many pounds of vegetables does a farmer have if he has 2 sacks of each? Solution: def solution():
    #A sack of onions weighs 50 pounds
    onions_weight = 50
    #A sack of carrots weighs 20 pounds
    carrots_weight = 20
    #A sack of potatoes weighs 30 pounds
    potatoes_weight = 30
    #A sack of cabbages weighs 40 pounds
    cabbages_weight = 40
    #A sack of radishes weighs 10 pounds
    radishes_weight = 10
    #A sack of beets weighs 15 pounds
    beets_weight = 15
    #The farmer has 2 sacks of each
    num_sacks_each = 2
    #The answer is
    result = (onions_weight + carrots_weight + potatoes_weight + cabbages_weight + radishes_weight + beets_weight) * num_sacks_each
    return result

### Response: Question: The 3rd grade class has 20 students. 1/5 of the students are in the after-school chess club. 1/3 of the students are in the after-school soccer club. How many students are in neither the chess nor soccer club? Solution: def solution():
    #The 3rd grade class has 20 students
    students = 20
    #1/5 of the students are in the after-school chess club
    chess_club = students / 5
    #1/3 of the students are in the after-school soccer club
    soccer_club = students / 3
    #The answer is
    result = students - chess_club - soccer_club
    return result

### Response: Question: A candy shop sells lollipops, candy canes, and gummy bears. The lollipops cost $2 each, the candy canes cost $3 each, and the gummy bears cost $4 each. A customer buys 2 lollipops, 2 candy canes, and 2 gummy bears. How much money does the customer spend? Solution: def solution():
    #The lollipops cost $2 each
    lollipop_cost = 2
    #The candy canes cost $3 each
    candy_cane_cost = 3
    #The gummy bears cost $4 each
    gummy_bear_cost = 4
    #The customer buys 2 lollipops
    lollipops_bought = 2
    #2 lollipops cost
    lollipop_cost_total = lollipop_cost * lollipops_bought
    #The customer buys 2 candy canes
    candy_canes_bought = 2
    #2 candy canes cost
    candy_cane_cost_total = candy_cane_cost * candy_canes_bought
    #The customer buys 2 gummy bears
    gummy_bears_bought = 2
    #2 gummy bears cost
    gummy_bear_cost_total = gummy_bear_cost * gummy_bears_bought
    #The answer is
    result = lollipop_cost_total + candy_cane_cost_total + gummy_bear_cost_total
    return result

### Response: Question: A 20-ounce soda has 2.5 ounces of sugar. How much sugar is in a 12-ounce soda? Solution: def solution():
    #A 20-ounce soda has 2.5 ounces of sugar
    soda_size_large = 20
    soda_size_small = 12
    soda_sugar_large = 2.5
    soda_sugar_small = soda_sugar_large * (soda_size_small / soda_size_large)
    result = soda_sugar_small
    return result

    loaves_sold = 1000
    #They bake in batches of 20
    loaves_per_batch = 20
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_sold / loaves_per_batch
    return result

### Response: Question: A 20-foot by 20-foot room has 4 windows. Each window is 2 feet by 4 feet. What is the total area of the walls? Solution: def solution():
    #The room is 20 feet by 20 feet
    room_length = 20
    room_width = 20
    #The windows are 2 feet by 4 feet
    window_length = 2
    window_width = 4
    #The room area is
    room_area = room_length * room_width
    #The window area is
    window_area = window_length * window_width
    #The total window area is
    total_window_area = window_area * 4
    #The answer is
    result = room_area - total_window_area
    return result

### Response: Question: A baker bakes 12 pies. The baker sells 8 pies and each pie is cut into 8 slices. How many slices of pie does the baker have left? Solution: def solution():
    #The baker bakes 12 pies
    pies_baked = 12
    #They sell 8 pies
    pies_sold = 8
    #Each pie is cut into 8 slices
    slices_per_pie = 8
    #The baker has
    slices_left = pies_baked * slices_per_pie - pies_sold * slices_per_pie
    return slices_left

### Response: Question: 250 people were at the soccer game. 120 of them were from the visiting team. 100 of them were from the home team. The rest were fans. How many fans were there? Solution: def solution():
    #250 people were at the soccer game
    people_at_game = 250
    #120 of them were from the visiting team
    visiting_team = 120
    #100 of them were from the home team
    home_team = 100
    #The answer is
    result = people_at_game - visiting_team - home_team
    return result
