### Response: Question: A cafeteria has 200 students. 30% of the students buy a hamburger, and 20% of the students buy a hot dog. How many students did not buy a hamburger or a hot dog? Solution: def solution():
    #A cafeteria has 200 students
    students = 200
    #30% of the students buy a hamburger
    hamburger_students = students * 0.3
    #20% of the students buy a hot dog
    hotdog_students = students * 0.2
    #The answer is
    result = students - hamburger_students - hotdog_students
    return result

### Response: Question: A pizzeria has a buy-one-get-one-free offer. If a pizza costs $10, how much will 5 pizzas cost? Solution: def solution():
    #A pizza costs $10
    pizza_cost = 10
    #For every pizza you buy, you get one free
    pizza_free = 1
    #5 pizzas at $10 each cost
    pizzas_cost = 5 * pizza_cost
    #5 pizzas get you 5 free pizzas
    pizzas_free = 5 * pizza_free
    #The answer is
    result = pizzas_cost - pizzas_free
    return result

    return result

    return result

### Response: Question: 123456789 is a 9-digit number. If you add the 1st, 3rd, and 5th digits, you get 1 + 3 + 5 = <<1+3+5=9>>9. If you add the 2nd, 4th, 6th, and 7th digits, you get 2 + 4 + 6 + 7 = <<2+4+6+7=19>>19. If you add the 8th and 9th digits, you get 8 + 9 = <<8+9=17>>17. The sum of all the digits is 9 + 19 + 17 = <<9+19+17=45>>45. What is the 8th digit of 123456789? Solution: def solution():
    #The 8th and 9th digits sum to 17
    digit_8_9 = 17
    #The 2nd, 4th, 6th, and 7th digits sum to 19
    digit_2_4_6_7 = 19
    #The 1st, 3rd, and 5th digits sum to 9
    digit_1_3_5 = 9
    #The sum of all the digits is 45
    digit_sum = 45
    #The 8th digit is
    result = digit_8_9 - 9
    return result

    result = pepperoni_slices

### Response: Question: A soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards. 6 of the players are midfielders. The rest of the players are defenders. How many defenders are on the team? Solution: def solution():
    #A soccer team has 24 players
    players_total = 24
    #12 of the players are forwards
    players_forwards = 12
    #6 of the players are midfielders
    players_midfielders = 6
    #The rest of the players are defenders. The answer is
    players_defenders = players_total - players_forwards - players_midfielders
    return players_defenders

### Response: Question: The soccer team has 24 players. 12 of the players are forwards. 6 of the players are defenders. The rest of the players are goalies. How many goalies are there? Solution: def solution():
    #The soccer team has 24 players
    players = 24
    #12 of the players are forwards
    forwards = 12
    #6 of the players are defenders
    defenders = 6
    #The rest of the players are goalies
    goalies = players - forwards - defenders
    #The answer is
    result = goalies
    return result

### Response: Question: The bakery sells 100 loaves of bread on Monday. They sell 50 more loaves of bread on Tuesday. On Wednesday, they sell 50% more loaves of bread than on Tuesday. How many loaves of bread did they sell by the end of Wednesday? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery sells 100 loaves of bread on Monday
    loaves_monday = 100
    #They sell 50 more loaves of bread on Tuesday
    loaves_tuesday = 50
    #On Wednesday, they sell 50% more loaves of bread than on Tuesday
    loaves_wednesday = loaves_tuesday * 1.5
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_monday + loaves_tuesday + loaves_wednesday
    return result

### Response: Question: The bakers at the Beverly Hills Bakery baked 200 loaves of bread on Monday morning. They sold 93 loaves in the morning and 39 loaves in the afternoon. A grocery store returned 6 unsold loaves. How many loaves of bread did they have left? Solution: def solution():

    #They sold 93 in the morning and 39 in the afternoon
    loaves_sold_morning=93

    #The grocery store returned 6 loaves
    loaves_returned = 6
    #The answer is

    return result

### Response: Question: A 20-foot by 20-foot room has 4 windows. Each window is 4 feet by 6 feet. What is the total area of the walls? Solution: def solution():
    #The room is 20 feet by 20 feet
    room_length = 20
    room_width = 20
    #The windows are 4 feet by 6 feet
    window_length = 4
    window_width = 6
    #The area of the room is
    room_area = room_length * room_width
    #The area of the windows is
    window_area = window_length * window_width
    #The total area of the windows is
    total_window_area = window_area * 4
    #The answer is
    result = room_area - total_window_area
    return result

    rough_cut_2by4_height = 4
    #After it is planed smooth, it is 1.5 inches by 3.5 inches.

    planed_2by4_height = 3.5

    rough_cut_2by4_weight = 20
    #The volume of a 120-inch long, rough-cut 2-by-4 is
    rough_cut_2by4_volume = 120 * rough_cut_2by4_width * rough_cut_2by4_height
    #The volume of a 120-inch long, planed 2-by-4 is
    planed_2by4_volume = 120 * planed_2by4_width * planed_2by4_height
    #The weight of a 120-inch long,

### Response: Question: A sack of onions weighs 50 pounds. A sack of carrots weighs 30 pounds. A sack of potatoes weighs 40 pounds. A sack of beans weighs 20 pounds. How much do 2 sacks of onions, 2 sacks of carrots, 2 sacks of potatoes, and 2 sacks of beans weigh? Solution: def solution():
    #A sack of onions weighs 50 pounds
    onions_weight = 50
    #A sack of carrots weighs 30 pounds
    carrots_weight = 30
    #A sack of potatoes weighs 40 pounds
    potatoes_weight = 40
    #A sack of beans weighs 20 pounds
    beans_weight = 20
    #2 sacks of onions weigh
    onions_two_sacks = 2 * onions_weight
    #2 sacks of carrots weigh
    carrots_two_sacks = 2 * carrots_weight
    #2 sacks of potatoes weigh
    potatoes_two_sacks = 2 * potatoes_weight
    #2 sacks of beans weigh
    beans_two_sacks = 2 * beans_weight
    #The answer is
    result = onions_two_sacks + carrots_two_sacks + potatoes_two_sacks + beans_two_sacks
    return result

### Response: Question: A bakery makes 1200 loaves of bread. 200 loaves are put in the display case. 400 loaves are put in the freezer. How many loaves of bread are left? Solution: def solution():
    #The bakery made 1200 loaves
    loaves_made = 1200
    #200 loaves were put in the display case
    loaves_display = 200
    #400 loaves were put in the freezer
    loaves_freezer = 400
    #The answer is
    result = loaves_made - loaves_display - loaves_freezer
    return result

### Response: Question: The total number of students in a school is 1500. 1/3 of the students are in the 10th grade. How many students are not in the 10th grade? Solution: def solution():
    #The total number of students is 1500
    students_total = 1500
    #1/3 of the students are in the 10th grade
    students_10th_grade = students_total / 3
    #The answer is
    result = students_total - students_10th_grade
    return result

### Response: Question: A warehouse has 10000 square feet of storage space. It has 5000 square feet of refrigerated storage space. How much is the non-refrigerated storage space in square feet? Solution: def solution():
    #The warehouse has 10000 square feet of storage space
    warehouse_storage = 10000
    #It has 5000 square feet of refrigerated storage space
    refrigerated_storage = 5000
    #The answer is
    result = warehouse_storage - refrigerated_storage
    return result
